331_CD ._. Appropriations_NNP ._. -_: -_: Appropriations--a_NNP form_NN of_IN budget_NN

entity_NN ,_, or_CC donated_VBD to_TO the_DT entity_NN ._. Therefore_RB ,_, appropriations_NNS provide_VBP
an_DT other_JJ financing_NN source_NN instead_RB of_IN a_DT revenue_NN ._.

SUMMARY_NNP
This_DT Statement_NNP establishes_VBZ standards_NNS for_IN reporting_VBG on_IN the_DT
Federal_NNP Government_NNP 's_POS stewardship_NN over_IN 1_LS )_) certain_JJ resources_NNS

Stewardship_NNP resources_NNS are_VBP investments_NNS by_IN the_DT Federal_NNP Government_NNP

STEWARDSHIP_NNP AND_CC THE_DT REPORTING_NNP OBJECTIVES_NNP


7_CD ._.
"_'' Financial_NNP position_NN "_'' is_VBZ a_DT representation_NN of_IN an_DT entity_NN 's_POS
economic_JJ resources_NNS and_CC the_DT claims_NNS on_IN those_DT resources_NNS as_IN of_IN a_DT
particular_JJ date_NN ._. In_IN the_DT private_JJ sector_NN ,_, the_DT principal_JJ objective_NN of_IN
reporting_VBG on_IN financial_JJ position_NN is_VBZ to_TO assess_VB the_DT viability_NN of_IN the_DT
entity_NN ,_, the_DT business_NN firm_NN ,_, and_CC its_PRP$ potential_JJ

8_CD ._.
Assessing_NNP the_DT overall_JJ performance_NN of_IN the_DT Federal_NNP
Government_NNP is_VBZ not_RB exclusively_RB a_DT matter_NN of_IN comparing_VBG revenue_NN and_CC
expense_NN ,_, or_CC its_PRP$ accumulated_VBN assets_NNS and_CC liabilities_NNS ._.


9_CD ._.
The_DT Federal_NNP Government_NNP 's_POS viability_NN and_CC perpetuity_NN are_VBP
assumed_VBN ._. It_PRP has_VBZ unique_JJ access_NN to_TO financial_JJ resources_NNS and_CC financing_NN ,_,
and_CC the_DT power_NN to_TO tax_VB ,_, to_TO borrow_VB ,_, and_CC to_TO create_VB money_NN ._. For_IN the_DT
Federal_NNP Government_NNP ,_, financial_JJ performance_NN is_VBZ a_DT vital_JJ issue_NN ,_, but_CC
traditional_JJ financial_JJ measures_NNS provide_VBP data_NNS that_WDT are_VBP appropriate_JJ
for_IN assessing_VBG only_RB some_DT ,_, not_RB all_DT ,_, of_IN the_DT responsibilities_NNS for_IN which_WDT
the_DT Government_NNP should_MD be_VB held_VBN accountable_JJ ._. Since_IN it_PRP exists_VBZ not_RB to_TO
make_VB a_DT profit_NN but_CC to_TO serve_VB the_DT needs_NNS of_IN the_DT citizens_NNS and_CC to_TO promote_VB
the_DT general_JJ welfare_NN of_IN the_DT Nation_NNP ,_, other_JJ measures_NNS of_IN accountability_NN
need_VBP to_TO be_VB used_VBN ._. Measures_NNS of_IN accountability_NN are_VBP to_TO be_VB reported_VBN for_IN
elements_NNS that_WDT are_VBP defined_VBN as_IN stewardship_NN property_NN ,_, plant_NN ,_, and_CC
equipment_NN (_( PP_NNP &_CC E_NNP )_) ;_: stewardship_NN investments_NNS ;_: and_CC stewardship_NN
responsibilities_NNS ._. These_DT elements_NNS of_IN stewardship_NN exist_VB because_IN the_DT
Federal_NNP Government_NNP is_VBZ dissimilar_JJ to_TO industrial_JJ and_CC commercial_JJ

Financial_NNP Condition_NNP
10_CD ._. The_DT measures_NNS of_IN accountability_NN mentioned_VBN above_IN help_NN to_TO
portray_VB the_DT Government_NNP 's_POS "_'' financial_JJ condition_NN ._. "_'' Financial_JJ condition_NN
is_VBZ a_DT broader_JJR and_CC more_RBR forward-looking_JJ concept_NN than_IN is_VBZ financial_JJ
position_NN ._. Financial_JJ condition_NN allows_VBZ an_DT assessment_NN of_IN an_DT entity_NN on_IN
the_DT basis_NN of_IN additional_JJ data_NNS that_WDT could_MD include_VB financial_JJ and_CC
nonfinancial_JJ information_NN about_IN current_JJ conditions_NNS ._. These_DT additional_JJ
data_NN provide_VBP a_DT more_RBR complete_JJ indication_NN of_IN performance_NN ._. In_IN some_DT
cases_NNS ,_, it_PRP may_MD be_VB necessary_JJ to_TO present_VB and_CC characterize_VB financial_JJ
data_NNS in_IN ways_NNS that_WDT differ_VBP from_IN traditional_JJ financial_JJ reporting_NN and_CC
to_TO supplement_VB traditional_JJ data_NNS with_IN nonfinancial_JJ data_NNS ._. In_IN other_JJ
cases_NNS ,_, it_PRP may_MD be_VB necessary_JJ to_TO rely_VB almost_RB entirely_RB on_IN nonfinancial_JJ
data_NNS to_TO provide_VB a_DT more_RBR complete_JJ presentation_NN of_IN entity_NN performance_NN ._.
Moreover_RB ,_, assessment_NN of_IN financial_JJ condition_NN could_MD include_VB analysis_NN
of_IN trends_NNS ,_, demands_NNS ,_, commitments_NNS ,_, events_NNS ,_, and_CC uncertainties_NNS ._. 4_LS
Stewardship_NNP PP_NNP &_CC E_NNP
11_CD ._. "_'' Stewardship_NNP PP_NNP &_CC E_NNP "_'' consists_VBZ of_IN items_NNS whose_WP$ physical_JJ
properties_NNS resemble_VBP those_DT of_IN general_JJ PP_NNP &_CC E_NNP traditionally_RB
capitalized_VBD in_IN financial_JJ statements_NNS ._. However_RB ,_, the_DT nature_NN of_IN these_DT
Federal_NNP physical_JJ assets_NNS that_WDT are_VBP classified_VBN as_IN stewardship_NN PP_NNP &_CC E_NNP
differ_VBP from_IN general_JJ PP_NNP &_CC E_NNP in_IN that_DT their_PRP$ values_NNS may_MD be_VB
indeterminable_JJ or_CC may_MD have_VB little_JJ meaning_NN (_( for_IN example_NN ,_, museum_NN
collections_NNS ,_, monuments_NNS ,_, assets_NNS acquired_VBN in_IN the_DT formation_NN of_IN the_DT
nation_NN )_) or_CC that_IN allocating_VBG the_DT cost_NN of_IN such_JJ assets_NNS (_( for_IN example_NN ,_,
military_JJ weapons_NNS systems_NNS and_CC space_NN exploration_NN hardware_NN )_) to_TO
